< Text>
I truly wish I could review less than a 1 star. I don't think I've ever been handeled as rudely at any nail salon I've been to compared to here.

I come in at around 11:30 I see every workers pretty busy, it's understandable it's Saturday morning. I ask John how long the wait will be he says 30 minutes I say okay well I'll go wait in my car, since there aren't any seats available (there were about 3-4 school aged children). I had asked should I tell you what I'm getting done so I can have my place held. He said no it's fine come back 30 minutes.

I came back 25 minutes later (wanting to catch time). I had to be in San Francisco at a certain time. I see they're still busy. I wait for another almost hr before being seen. During that though 2 women had came in and been seen. I also made sure I told him well I'm getting my feet done to, he said no problem I'll see you soon.

Normally when salons are busy and you're doing your feet as well they'll have you soak your feet while you're waiting I didn't get that.

Fast forward he finally sees me after waiting as long as I did and I told him I only need to get 2 fingers fixed. He tries to upsell me and says it'll be the same price if I just take off all your nails and give you a new set (I know that's not true). I go are you sure it's just 2 fingers that need to be changed plus I'm cautious on time I've already waited far longer than I was told and anticipated. He reassures me says it'll be $40 for a new set with gel. I did the math and it was at least $10 off. Whatever I didn't want to argue with him. He proceeds to trim my nail down to make it easier to take my nail off he says.

He starts to grab a nail to wedge between my nail and acrylic. Mind you the acrylic and the fake nail are tacked on with glue and forcing that off hurts. I've worked with John a couple times at another shop he worked at. He's did this method on me before and it hurts extremely bad. I told him could he please just buff it off, he gets very defensive and says no, I said well the way you're doing right now hurts really bad I remember the last time.

John catches a real nasty attitude and says no the other way is bad for your nails I'm not doing it that way, mind you every other nail shop I've went to does it the way I mentioned, they've never hurt me and it's faster as well. He states well why can't you go there, lol dude I just waited over an hr I don't have time to go anywhere else now.

He then tells me he can't do my nails, KEEP IN MIND HES ALREADY CUT MY NAILS, so I would be walking out with uneven short acrylic nails that weren't buffed or shaped. I was really upset I told him I waited an hour and I'm not going to walk out of this salon without the fakr nails at least off since he already cut all of them. He said you don't have to pay me you can go. I asked well can anyone else in your shop do it the way I asked he said no they can't they only do it this way. I said okay well as stated before I'm not leaving until you take these nails off, I have somewhere to be I cannot just leave here after you've made them unpresenstable. With just as much attitude and disdain he says fine we'll do it your way if that's what you like whatever saves me time anyway good that's great.

He turns the machine on full blast and starts going crazy on my nails not in a way that I've ever seen, all while under his breath saying whatever we'll do it your way I don't care, I'm scared because like I said machine is on full blast he's not being careful nicked my skin. He finally does one uneven round on my nails and gets ready to go again I get up ready to leave.

He gets up like you're not going to pay me?! I told him of course not if he doesn't want to do my nails that's fine. But I'm not going to have him unprofessionally do my nails while he's talking directly infront of me under his breath about how he doesn't want to do my nails.

I leave he walks after me, I continue walking not looking back and he called me the mf'er.

There's other great shops in vallejo like Nice Nails that I can give my money to</Text>

Last night we went to Jazeera Market to buy Half & Half for our morning coffee & two Snickers candy bars.

The Snickers were either old or had been overheated so the chocolate was white & crumbly. We ate them anyway.

However when I opened the first two of them this morning, they were spoiled. So we threw them away & drank our coffee black. Grrr.

<rating>1<//rating>< text>
My family decided to give this place a try because of the high reviews.....It was dreadful. Our first pizza was burned, black edges and very dark brown crust.
When we called they said they would make us another one. When I picked up the new pizza the were completely unapologetic and condescending, opening it in my face and asking "is this one okay?" ( If you dont know the answer to that question and thought the first was good, then you shouldn't be making Pizza)
Sadly the (good) pizza wasnt good either. The crust was still overdone, dry, and tasted kind of burned. There was too much cheese distributed unevenly and caked together, but the worst part was the sauce.
I love spicy food, but you shouldnt make your base sauce too spicy that kids cant eat it, if somebody wants spicy pizza they can add red pepper.
Like some other reviews mentioned, the sauce was way too spicy for my child to eat. So after all the money spent, two trips, I still didnt have edible food for my family. TRASH, not going back.< /text>
